     2 
     3 const corsHeaders = {
     4   "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
     5   "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
     6 };
     7 
     8 Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
     9   if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    10     return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
    11   }
    12 
    13   if (req.method !== "POST") {
    14     return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });
    15   }
    16 
    17   let messages: Array<{ role: string; content: string }>;
    18   let enableThinking = false;
    19 
    20   try {
    21     const body = await req.json();
    22     messages = body.messages;
    23     if (!messages || !Array.isArray(messages) || messages.length === 0) {
    24       throw new Error("Missing or invalid messages");
    25     }
    26     if (body.enable_thinking !== undefined) {
    27       enableThinking = Boolean(body.enable_thinking);
    28     }
    29   } catch (err) {
    30     return new Response(
    31       JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request body: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
    32       { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    33     );
    34   }
    35 
    36   const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
    37   if (!apiKey) {
    38     return new Response(
    39       JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error: missing API key" }),
    40       { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    41     );
    42   }
    43 
    44   const upstream = await fetch(
    45     "https://app-bgc5z86utjwh-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
    46     {
    47       method: "POST",
    48       headers: {
    49         "Content-Type": "application/json",
    50         "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    51       },
    52       body: JSON.stringify({ messages, enable_thinking: enableThinking }),
    53     }
    54   );
    55 
    56   if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    57     const errText = await upstream.text();
    58     return new Response(errText, {
    59       status: upstream.status,
    60       headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    61     });
    62   }
    63 
    64   if (!upstream.ok || !upstream.body) {
    65     return new Response(
    66       JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
    67       { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    68     );
    69   }
    70 
    71   return new Response(upstream.body, {
    72     headers: {
    73       ...corsHeaders,
    74       "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
    75       "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
    76       "Connection": "keep-alive",

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/src/lib/sse.ts:
     1 // SSE 流式请求工具（文心大模型）
     2 
     3 import ky, {
     4   type KyResponse,
     5   type AfterResponseHook,
     6   type NormalizedOptions,
     7 } from 'ky';
     8 import { createParser, type EventSourceParser } from 'eventsource-parser';
     9 
    10 export interface SSEOptions {
    11   onData: (data: string) => void;
    12   onEvent?: (event: unknown) => void;
    13   onCompleted?: (error?: Error) => void;
    14   onAborted?: () => void;
    15 }
    16 
    17 export function createSSEHook(options: SSEOptions): AfterResponseHook {
    18   const hook: AfterResponseHook = async (
    19     request: Request,
    20     _options: NormalizedOptions,
    21     response: KyResponse
    22   ) => {
    23     if (!response.ok || !response.body) return;
    24 
    25     let completed = false;
    26     const finish = (error?: Error): void => {
    27       if (completed) return;
    28       completed = true;
    29       options.onCompleted?.(error);
    30     };
    31 
    32     const reader = response.body.getReader();
    33     const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf8');
    34     const parser: EventSourceParser = createParser({
    35       onEvent: (event) => {
    36         if (!event.data) return;
    37         options.onEvent?.(event);
    38         for (const chunk of event.data.split('\\ ')) {
    39           options.onData(chunk);
    40         }
    41       },
    42     });
    43 
    44     const read = (): void => {
    45       reader
    46         .read()
    47         .then((result) => {
    48           if (result.done) {
    49             finish();
    50             return;
    51           }
    52           parser.feed(decoder.decode(result.value, { stream: true }));
    53           read();
    54         })
    55         .catch((error) => {
    56           if (request.signal.aborted) {
    57             options.onAborted?.();
    58             return;
    59           }
    60           finish(error as Error);
    61         });
    62     };
    63 
    64     read();
    65     return response;
    66   };
    67 
    68   return hook;
    69 }
    70 
    71 export interface StreamRequestOptions {
    72   functionUrl: string;
    73   requestBody: unknown;
    74   supabaseAnonKey: string;
    75   onData: (data: string) => void;
    76   onComplete: () => void;
    77   onError: (error: Error) => void;
    78   signal?: AbortSignal;
    79 }
    80 
    81 export async function sendStreamRequest(options: StreamRequestOptions): Promise<void> {
    82   const { functionUrl, requestBody, supabaseAnonKey, onData, onComplete, onError, signal } = options;
    83 
    84   const sseHook = createSSEHook({
    85     onData,
    86     onCompleted: (error?: Error) => {
    87       if (error) onError(error);
    88       else onComplete();
    89     },
    90     onAborted: () => console.log('请求已中断'),
    91   });
    92 
    93   try {
    94     await ky.post(functionUrl, {
    95       json: requestBody,
    96       headers: {
    97         Authorization: `Bearer ${supabaseAnonKey}`,
    98         apikey: supabaseAnonKey,
    99         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   100       },
   101       signal,
   102       timeout: 60000,
   103       hooks: { afterResponse: [sseHook] },
   104     });
   105   } catch (error) {
   106     if (!signal?.aborted) onError(error as Error);
   107   }
   108 }
   109 
   110 /** 解析 SSE data 帧，提取文心大模型增量内容 */
   111 export function parseWenxinChunk(data: string): string {
   112   if (data === '[DONE]') return '';
   113   try {
   114     const parsed = JSON.parse(data);
   115     return parsed.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content ?? '';
   116   } catch {
   117     return '';
   118   }
   119 }
   120

     1 // AI 辅助功能 Hook（基于文心大模型）
     2 
     3 import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
     4 import { sendStreamRequest, parseWenxinChunk } from '@/lib/sse';
     5 
     6 const SUPABASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL as string;
     7 const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY as string;
     8 
     9 const FUNCTION_URL = `${SUPABASE_URL}/functions/v1/wenxin-text-generation`;
    10 
    11 /** 流式生成文本，返回完整内容 */
    12 async function generateText(
    13   messages: Array<{ role: 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system'; content: string }>,
    14   onChunk: (chunk: string) => void,
    15   signal: AbortSignal
    16 ): Promise<string> {
    17   let full = '';
    18   await sendStreamRequest({
    19     functionUrl: FUNCTION_URL,
    20     requestBody: { messages },
    21     supabaseAnonKey: SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
    22     onData: (data) => {
    23       const chunk = parseWenxinChunk(data);
    24       if (chunk) {
    25         full += chunk;
    26         onChunk(chunk);
    27       }
    28     },
    29     onComplete: () => {},
    30     onError: (err) => { throw err; },
    31     signal,
    32   });
    33   return full;
    34 }
    35 
    36 // ===== AI 摘要 Hook =====
    37 export interface UseAiSummaryResult {
    38   summary: string;
    39   loading: boolean;
    40   generate: (context: string) => Promise<void>;
    41   clear: () => void;
    42 }
    43 
    44 export function useAiSummary(): UseAiSummaryResult {
    45   const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    46   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    47   const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
    48 
    49   const generate = useCallback(async (context: string) => {
    50     abortRef.current?.abort();
    51     abortRef.current = new AbortController();
    52     setSummary('');
    53     setLoading(true);
    54     try {
    55       await generateText(
    56         [
    57           {
    58             role: 'system',
    59             content: '你是一个 GitHub 项目助手，擅长简洁总结 Issue 和 PR 内容。',
    60           },
    61           {
    62             role: 'user',
    63             content: `请用不超过100字，简洁总结以下内容的核心要点（直接输出摘要，不要引言）：\n\n${context}`,
    64           },
    65         ],
    66         (chunk) => setSummary((prev) => prev + chunk),
    67         abortRef.current.signal
    68       );
    69     } catch (err) {
    70       if ((err as Error)?.name !== 'AbortError') throw err;
    71     } finally {
    72       setLoading(false);
    73     }
    74   }, []);
    75 
    76   const clear = useCallback(() => {
    77     abortRef.current?.abort();
    78     setSummary('');
    79     setLoading(false);
    80   }, []);
    81 
    82   return { summary, loading, generate, clear };
    83 }
    84 
    85 // ===== AI 回复建议 Hook =====
    86 export interface UseAiSuggestionsResult {
    87   suggestions: string[];
    88   loading: boolean;
    89   generate: (context: string) => Promise<void>;
    90   clear: () => void;
    91 }
    92 
    93 export function useAiSuggestions(): UseAiSuggestionsResult {
    94   const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState<string[]>([]);
    95   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    96   const [rawBuffer, setRawBuffer] = useState('');
    97   const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
    98 
    99   const generate = useCallback(async (context: string) => {
   100     abortRef.current?.abort();
   101     abortRef.current = new AbortController();
   102     setSuggestions([]);
   103     setRawBuffer('');
   104     setLoading(true);
   105     try {
   106       const full = await generateText(
   107         [
   108           {
   109             role: 'system',
   110             content: '你是一个 GitHub 项目助手，帮助用户快速回复 Issue 或 PR。',
   111           },
   112           {
   113             role: 'user',
   114             content: `根据以下 GitHub Issue/PR 内容，生成 3 条简洁的回复候选（每条不超过50字）。\n格式要求：每条回复单独一行，以"1. ""2. ""3. "开头。\n\n内容：\n${context}`,
   115           },
   116         ],
   117         (chunk) => setRawBuffer((prev) => prev + chunk),
   118         abortRef.current.signal
   119       );
   120       // 解析编号列表
   121       const lines = full
   122         .split('\n')
   123         .map((l) => l.replace(/^[\d]+[.、。]\s*/, '').trim())
   124         .filter((l) => l.length > 0)
   125         .slice(0, 3);
   126       setSuggestions(lines);
   127     } catch (err) {
   128       if ((err as Error)?.name !== 'AbortError') throw err;
   129     } finally {
   130       setLoading(false);
   131       setRawBuffer('');
   132     }
   133   }, []);
   134 
   135   const clear = useCallback(() => {
   136     abortRef.current?.abort();
   137     setSuggestions([]);
   138     setLoading(false);
   139     setRawBuffer('');
   140   }, []);
   141 
   142   // 流式生成时实时解析部分结果
   143   const liveSuggestions = suggestions.length > 0 ? suggestions : (
   144     rawBuffer
   145       ? rawBuffer.split('\n').map((l) => l.replace(/^[\d]+[.、。]\s*/, '').trim()).filter((l) => l.length > 0).slice(0, 3)
   146       : []
   147   );
   148 
   149   return { suggestions: liveSuggestions, loading, generate, clear };
   150 }

     9   base: "./",
    10   plugins: [

    12     svgr({

    28     // 静态资源统一放 assets/ 目录

    30     chunkSizeWarningLimit: 2000,
    31     // 关闭 <link rel="modulepreload">：
    32     // WebView 以 file:// 加载时，modulepreload 会触发额外的文件请求，
    33     // 在部分 Android 版本中会因 file:// 跨资源限制而静默失败，导致白屏/黑屏
    34     modulePreload: false,
    35     rollupOptions: {
    36       output: {
    37         // 不做 manualChunks 拆分：
    38         // file:// 协议下，动态 import() 跨 chunk 文件在部分 WebView 版本中

    40         // 不拆包后，所有代码合并进少量静态 chunk，WebView 可以顺序加载，无动态 import 权限问题。

SkillObservation(content='Base directory for this skill: /workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/.skills/wenxin-text-generation\n\n## 能力概述\n\n使用百度文心大模型（ERNIE 4.5 Turbo）进行对话式文本生成，支持内容生成、语言润色、摘要提炼、信息提取、翻译等场景。\n\n| 项目 | 值 |\n|------|----|\n| Endpoint | `POST https://app-bgc5z86utjwh-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions` |\n| 响应模式 | SSE 流式（Server-Sent Events） |\n| 认证模式 | `platform_managed`（密钥由平台注入） |\n| 上下文限制 | 32k token 总长度，27k token 单次输入 |\n| 支持平台 | Web、MiniProgram、App、Task |\n\nAuth Header 为 `X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer ${INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY}`（注意不是标准的 `Authorization`）。\n\n\n**多平台关键差异：**\n\n| 平台 | 流式处理方式 | 核心依赖 |\n|------|-------------|---------|\n| Web | `ky` + `eventsource-parser` SSE Hook | `ky@^1.2.3`, `eventsource-parser@^3.0.3` |\n| MiniProgram | `miaoda-taro-utils` 的 `sendChatStream` | `miaoda-taro-utils@^0.0.4` |\n| App | `expo/fetch` + `eventsource-parser` 手动解析 SSE 流 | `expo/fetch`（内置）, `eventsource-parser@^3.0.3`, `react-native-marked` |\n\n**响应数据格式（流式每帧）：**\n\n```json\n{\n  "id": "as-9ki4hm6kkp",\n  "choices": [\n    {\n      "index": 0,\n      "delta": {\n        "role": "assistant",\n        "content": "您好！"\n      },\n      "finish_reason": null,\n      "flag": 0\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n内容提取：`choices[0].delta.content`\n\n---\n\n## 生成期用法（Agent 直接调用）\n\n直接从 Agent 脚本调用上游 SSE 流式接口，适合生成期任务处理。\n\n详细参数表、完整生成期代码及 Edge Function 实现见 [references/chat-completions-api.md](references/chat-completions-api.md)。\n\n---\n\n## 生成后用法（应用内通过 Edge Function 调用）\n\n应用内通过 Supabase Edge Function 代理调用，Edge Function 负责持有 `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` 并将上游 SSE 流透传给前端。\n\n**平台差异说明：**\n\n| 平台 | Edge Function | 前端调用方式 |\n|------|--------------|-------------|\n| Web | 同一个 Edge Function（SSE proxy） | `ky` + `eventsource-parser` SSE Hook |\n| MiniProgram | 同一个 Edge Function（SSE proxy） | `miaoda-taro-utils` 的 `sendChatStream`，`appId` 填空字符串 |\n| App | 同一个 Edge Function（SSE proxy） | `expo/fetch` + `eventsource-parser` 手动解析 SSE，`react-native-marked` 渲染 |\n\n详细 Edge Function 代码及各平台前端调用代码见 [references/chat-completions-api.md](references/chat-completions-api.md)。', Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/.github/workflows/deploy.yml:
     1 # GitHub Pages 自动部署 + Android APK 构建 + Release 发布工作流
     2 # 推送到 main 分支时：
     3 #   1. 构建 Web 应用（dist/）
     4 #   2. 部署到 GitHub Pages
     5 #   3. 打包签名 Release APK（WebView 壳 + dist/ 资源）
     6 #   4. 自动创建 GitHub Release 并上传 APK
     7 #
     8 # ── Secrets 配置说明 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9 # 仓库 Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions 中可配置：
    10 #
    11 #   【签名 Secrets（可选）】
    12 #   RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64   release.keystore 文件的 base64 内容
    13 #   RELEASE_KEY_ALIAS         密钥别名（默认 github-manager）
    14 #   RELEASE_STORE_PASSWORD    keystore 密码
    15 #   RELEASE_KEY_PASSWORD      key 密码
    16 #
    17 #   【自动持久化 Secret（可选，强烈推荐）】
    18 #   GH_PAT  具有 "repo" 权限的 Personal Access Token（PAT）
    19 #           首次构建时 CI 自动生成 Keystore，并通过 GH_PAT 将其写回
    20 #           上方 4 个签名 Secrets，之后所有构建复用同一证书，
    21 #           支持跨版本覆盖安装。
    22 #           创建 PAT：GitHub → Settings → Developer settings →
    23 #           Personal access tokens → Generate new token（classic）
    24 #           勾选 repo 权限后生成，填入 GH_PAT Secret。
    25 #
    26 #   【零配置模式】
    27 #   以上 Secrets 均不填时，CI 仍可正常构建，但每次生成不同临时证书，
    28 #   安装后无法被下一个构建版本覆盖安装。
    29 # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    30 name: Deploy & Build APK
    31 
    32 on:
    33   push:
    34     branches: [main]
    35   workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发
    36 
    37 # GITHUB_TOKEN 权限
    38 permissions:
    39   contents: write   # 创建 GitHub Release 需要 write 权限
    40   pages: write
    41   id-token: write
    42 
    43 # 同组并发：新部署取消旧部署（仅影响 Pages，APK 构建不受影响）
    44 concurrency:
    45   group: pages
    46   cancel-in-progress: true
    47 
    48 # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    49 jobs:
    50 
    51   # ── Job 1：构建 Web 应用 ───────────────────────────────────────
    52   build-web:
    53     name: 构建 Web 应用
    54     runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    55     steps:
    56       - name: 检出代码
    57         uses: actions/checkout@v4
    58 
    59       - name: 安装 pnpm
    60         uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
    61         with:
    62           version: 9
    63 
    64       - name: 设置 Node.js
    65         uses: actions/setup-node@v4
    66         with:
    67           node-version: 20
    68 
    69       - name: 安装依赖
    70         run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
    71 
    72       - name: 构建 Web 应用（注入版本号）
    73         env:
    74           # 版本号格式 1.0.<run_number>，与 APK versionName 保持一致
    75           VITE_APP_VERSION: "1.0.${{ github.run_number }}"
    76         run: pnpm exec vite build
    77 
    78       - name: 上传 Web 构建产物（供后续 Job 使用）
    79         uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
    80         with:
    81           name: web-dist
    82           path: dist
    83           retention-days: 1
    84 
    85       - name: 配置 GitHub Pages
    86         uses: actions/configure-pages@v5
    87 
    88       - name: 上传 Pages 产物
    89         uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
    90         with:
    91           path: dist
    92 
    93   # ── Job 2：部署到 GitHub Pages ─────────────────────────────────
    94   deploy-pages:
    95     name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
    96     needs: build-web
    97     runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    98     environment:
    99       name: github-pages
   100       url: ${{ steps.deployment.outputs.page_url }}
   101     steps:
   102       - name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
   103         id: deployment
   104         uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4
   105 
   106   # ── Job 3：构建签名 Release APK 并发布 ────────────────────────
   107   build-apk:
   108     name: 构建 Android APK 并发布 Release
   109     needs: build-web
   110     runs-on: ubuntu-latest
   111     steps:
   112       - name: 检出代码（含 android/ 项目源码）
   113         uses: actions/checkout@v4
   114 
   115       - name: 下载 Web 构建产物
   116         uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
   117         with:
   118           name: web-dist
   119           path: dist
   120 
   121       - name: 将 Web 资源复制到 Android assets
   122         run: |
   123           mkdir -p android/app/src/main/assets
   124           cp -r dist/. android/app/src/main/assets/
   125 
   126       - name: 设置 JDK 17
   127         uses: actions/setup-java@v4
   128         with:
   129           java-version: '17'
   130           distribution: 'temurin'
   131 
   132       - name: 设置 Gradle 8.7
   133         uses: gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3
   134         with:
   135           gradle-version: '8.7'
   136           cache-read-only: false
   137 
   138       - name: 生成 local.properties
   139         run: echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > android/local.properties
   140 
   141       - name: 接受 Android SDK 许可证
   142         run: |
   143           yes | $ANDROID_HOME/cmdline-tools/latest/bin/sdkmanager --licenses 2>/dev/null || true
   144 
   145       # ── 签名配置 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   146       # 优先使用仓库 Secret 中的稳定 Release Keystore（支持跨版本覆盖安装）；
   147       # 未配置 Secret 时，用 keytool -genkeypair 自动生成临时 Keystore 并用于签名，
   148       # 使 APK 始终以 Release 模式构建（而非 Debug），但该临时证书每次构建都会变化，
   149       # 无法跨不同构建版本覆盖安装。如需稳定签名，请按注释说明配置 Secrets。
   150       - name: 配置 Release Keystore
   151         id: keystore
   152         env:
   153           RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64: ${{ secrets.RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64 }}
   154           RELEASE_KEY_ALIAS:       ${{ secrets.RELEASE_KEY_ALIAS }}
   155           RELEASE_STORE_PASSWORD:  ${{ secrets.RELEASE_STORE_PASSWORD }}
   156           RELEASE_KEY_PASSWORD:    ${{ secrets.RELEASE_KEY_PASSWORD }}
   157         run: |
   158           KEYSTORE_PATH="${GITHUB_WORKSPACE}/android/release.keystore"
   159 
   160           if [ -n "${RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64}" ]; then
   161             # ── 方案 A：使用仓库 Secret 中的稳定 Keystore ────────────
   162             echo "✅ 使用 Secret 中的 Release Keystore（支持覆盖安装）"
   163             echo "${RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64}" | base64 --decode > "${KEYSTORE_PATH}"
   164             STORE_PASS="${RELEASE_STORE_PASSWORD}"
   165             KEY_ALIAS_VAL="${RELEASE_KEY_ALIAS}"
   166             KEY_PASS="${RELEASE_KEY_PASSWORD}"
   167             echo "was_generated=false" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   168           else
   169             # ── 方案 B：Secret 未配置，用 keytool 自动生成临时 Keystore ─
   170             echo "⚠️  未检测到 RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64 Secret"
   171             echo "   正在使用 keytool -genkeypair 生成临时签名 Keystore..."
   172             echo "   ℹ️  若配置了 GH_PAT Secret，本次生成的证书将自动写入仓库"
   173             echo "      Secrets，后续构建将复用同一证书，支持覆盖安装。"
   174             echo "   📋  未配置 GH_PAT 时，临时证书每次重新生成，无法跨版本覆盖安装。"
   175 
   176             STORE_PASS="GithubManager@CI"
   177             KEY_ALIAS_VAL="github-manager"
   178             KEY_PASS="GithubManager@CI"
   179 
   180             keytool -genkeypair -v \
   181               -keystore "${KEYSTORE_PATH}" \
   182               -alias "${KEY_ALIAS_VAL}" \
   183               -keyalg RSA \
   184               -keysize 2048 \
   185               -validity 10000 \
   186               -storepass "${STORE_PASS}" \
   187               -keypass "${KEY_PASS}" \
   188               -dname "CN=GitHub Manager CI, OU=Build, O=CI, L=CN, S=CN, C=CN" \
   189               -noprompt
   190 
   191             echo "✅ 临时 Keystore 生成成功：${KEYSTORE_PATH}"
   192 
   193             # 将 base64 写入临时文件，供后续写入 Secrets 步骤使用
   194             base64 -w 0 "${KEYSTORE_PATH}" > /tmp/keystore_b64.txt
   195             echo "was_generated=true"                 >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   196             echo "keystore_b64_file=/tmp/keystore_b64.txt" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   197             echo "generated_alias=${KEY_ALIAS_VAL}"   >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   198             echo "generated_store_pass=${STORE_PASS}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   199             echo "generated_key_pass=${KEY_PASS}"     >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   200           fi
   201 
   202           echo "keystore_path=${KEYSTORE_PATH}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   203           echo "store_password=${STORE_PASS}"   >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   204           echo "key_alias=${KEY_ALIAS_VAL}"     >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   205           echo "key_password=${KEY_PASS}"       >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   206 
   207       # ── 将自动生成的 Keystore 写回仓库 Secrets（需要 GH_PAT）────────
   208       # 写入成功后，下次构建会走方案 A（稳定 Keystore），支持跨版本覆盖安装
   209       - name: 写入 Keystore 到仓库 Secrets
   210         if: steps.keystore.outputs.was_generated == 'true'
   211         env:
   212           GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GH_PAT }}
   213           B64_FILE: ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.keystore_b64_file }}
   214           GEN_ALIAS: ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.generated_alias }}
   215           GEN_STORE_PASS: ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.generated_store_pass }}
   216           GEN_KEY_PASS: ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.generated_key_pass }}
   217         run: |
   218           if [ -z "${GH_TOKEN}" ]; then
   219             echo "⚠️  未配置 GH_PAT Secret，跳过自动写入仓库 Secrets。"
   220             echo "   临时证书仅用于本次构建，下次构建仍会重新生成新证书。"
   221             echo ""
   222             echo "   📋  如需稳定签名（支持覆盖安装），请："
   223             echo "   1. GitHub → Settings → Developer settings →"
   224             echo "      Personal access tokens → Generate new token (classic)"
   225             echo "   2. 勾选 repo 权限 → 生成 Token"
   226             echo "   3. 将 Token 添加为仓库 Secret，名称：GH_PAT"
   227             echo "   4. 再次触发构建，CI 将自动完成后续配置"
   228           else
   229             echo "🔑  GH_PAT 可用，正在将 Keystore 写入仓库 Secrets..."
   230             REPO="${{ github.repository }}"
   231             gh secret set RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64  --body "$(cat ${B64_FILE})"  --repo "${REPO}"
   232             gh secret set RELEASE_KEY_ALIAS        --body "${GEN_ALIAS}"        --repo "${REPO}"
   233             gh secret set RELEASE_STORE_PASSWORD   --body "${GEN_STORE_PASS}"   --repo "${REPO}"
   234             gh secret set RELEASE_KEY_PASSWORD     --body "${GEN_KEY_PASS}"     --repo "${REPO}"
   235             echo "✅  4 个 Secrets 写入成功！"
   236             echo "   下次构建将使用稳定证书，支持跨版本覆盖安装。"
   237           fi
   238 
   239       # ── 构建签名 Release APK ───────────────────────────────────
   240       - name: 构建签名 Release APK
   241         working-directory: android
   242         env:
   243           VERSION_CODE:    ${{ github.run_number }}
   244           VERSION_NAME:    "1.0.${{ github.run_number }}"
   245           KEYSTORE_PATH:   ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.keystore_path }}
   246           STORE_PASSWORD:  ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.store_password }}
   247           KEY_ALIAS:       ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.key_alias }}
   248           KEY_PASSWORD:    ${{ steps.keystore.outputs.key_password }}
   249         run: gradle assembleRelease --no-daemon
   250 
   251       # ── 规范化 APK 文件名 ──────────────────────────────────────
   252       - name: 重命名 APK
   253         id: rename_apk
   254         run: |
   255           VERSION_NAME="1.0.${{ github.run_number }}"
   256           APK_NAME="github-manager-v${VERSION_NAME}.apk"
   257           # 始终使用 Release APK（两种签名方案均走 assembleRelease）
   258           cp "android/app/build/outputs/apk/release/app-release.apk" "${APK_NAME}"
   259           echo "apk_name=${APK_NAME}"       >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   260           echo "version_name=${VERSION_NAME}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   261 
   262       # ── 创建 GitHub Release 并上传 APK ────────────────────────
   263       - name: 创建 GitHub Release
   264         env:
   265           GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   266           RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64: ${{ secrets.RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64 }}
   267         run: |
   268           VERSION_NAME="${{ steps.rename_apk.outputs.version_name }}"
   269           APK_NAME="${{ steps.rename_apk.outputs.apk_name }}"
   270           TAG="v${VERSION_NAME}"
   271           COMMIT_SHA="${{ github.sha }}"
   272           SHORT_SHA="${COMMIT_SHA:0:7}"
   273 
   274           # 根据是否使用了稳定 Secret Keystore 生成不同的签名说明
   275           if [ -n "${RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64}" ]; then
   276             SIGN_NOTE="✅ **稳定 Release 签名**（可跨版本覆盖安装，正式分发）"
   277           else
   278             SIGN_NOTE="⚠️ **临时 Release 签名**（keytool 自动生成，本次构建可安装，但无法覆盖安装其他构建版本；配置 RELEASE_KEYSTORE_BASE64 Secret 后升级为稳定签名）"
   279           fi
   280 
   281           NOTES="## GitHub Manager ${TAG}
   282 
   283           **构建信息**
   284           - 版本号：\`${VERSION_NAME}\`（versionCode: \`${{ github.run_number }}\`）
   285           - 提交：[\`${SHORT_SHA}\`](${{ github.server_url }}/${{ github.repository }}/commit/${COMMIT_SHA})
   286           - 构建时间：$(date -u '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M UTC')
   287           - ${SIGN_NOTE}
   288 
   289           **安装方式**
   290           1. 下载下方 APK 文件到 Android 设备
   291           2. 允许「安装未知来源应用」后点击安装
   292           3. 如已安装旧版本，使用 Release 签名版本可直接覆盖安装（无需卸载）
   293 
   294           **系统要求**
   295           - Android 8.0（API 26）及以上"
   296 
   297           # 如同名 tag 已存在则先删除（workflow_dispatch 重复触发场景）
   298           gh release delete "${TAG}" --yes 2>/dev/null || true
   299           git push origin --delete "${TAG}" 2>/dev/null || true
   300 
   301           gh release create "${TAG}" \
   302             --title "GitHub Manager ${TAG}" \
   303             --notes "${NOTES}" \
   304             --latest \
   305             "${APK_NAME}"

```
  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    console.error("Missing INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error: missing API key. Please ensure it is set in Supabase Secrets." }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  console.log(`Processing AI request with ${messages.length} messages`);

  try {
    const upstream = await fetch(
      "https://app-bgc5z86utjwh-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
      {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/json",
          "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ messages, enable_thinking: enableThinking, stream: true }),
      }
    );

    if (!upstream.ok) {
      const errText = await upstream.text();
      console.error(`Upstream error: ${upstream.status} - ${errText}`);
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}`, details: errText }),
        { status: upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402 ? upstream.status : 502, 
          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
      );
    }

    if (!upstream.body) {
      console.error("Upstream returned empty body");
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: "Upstream returned empty body" }),
        { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
      );
    }

    return new Response(upstream.body, {
      headers: {
        ...corsHeaders,
        "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
        "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
        "Connection": "keep-alive",
        "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
      },
    });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(`Fetch error: ${(err as Error).message}`);
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Internal server error: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }
});
```

```
          {/* AI 回复建议 */}
          <div className="space-y-1.5">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium">回复建议</span>
              <Button
                variant="ghost"
                size="sm"
                className="h-6 px-2 text-xs text-primary hover:bg-primary/10 gap-1"
                onClick={() => {
                  const ctx = `PR 标题：${pr.title}\n描述：${pr.body || '（无描述）'}`;
                  aiSuggestions.generate(ctx).catch((err) => toast.error(`建议生成失败: ${err.message}`));
                }}
                disabled={aiSuggestions.loading}

```
